    <script>
        function loadScript(url, async, defer, crossorigin, type) {
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.src = url;
            if (async) {
                script.async = true;
            }
            if (defer) {
                script.defer = true;
            }
            if (crossorigin) {
                script.crossOrigin = 'anonymous';
            }
            if (type === 'head') {
                document.head.appendChild(script);
            } else {
                document.body.appendChild(script);
            }

        }
    </script>
